     <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript">
      $(function(){
      //電腦版date
      m_date = $('.container .topbg .date').text();
      m_date2 = $('.container .topbg .date2').text();
      //手機版date
      $('.topbg_m .date').html( m_date + '<small>/</small>' + m_date2 + '<span>每日五檔特賣</span>' );
      //回版頭
      jQuery("#gotop").click(function(){
        jQuery("html,body").stop(true,false).animate({scrollTop:0}); //設定回頁面頂端
        return false;
      });
      jQuery(window).scroll(function() {
        if ( jQuery(this).scrollTop() > 300){ //設定大於300px才顯示浮層
          jQuery('#gotop').fadeIn("fast");
        } else {
          jQuery('#gotop').stop().fadeOut("fast");
        }
      });
    });
    
    function clock(){
      var nowTime = new Date;
      var nowHours = nowTime.getHours();
      var nowMinutes = nowTime.getMinutes();
      var nowSecond = nowTime.getSeconds();
      
      var nextPosEndTime = $('#posTag1').find('.dateTime > .period > span').text().split('~')[1].split(' ')[1];
      var nextPosEndTimeHour = nextPosEndTime.split(':')[0];
      var nextPosEndTimeMinutes = nextPosEndTime.split(':')[1];
      
      var reHours = nextPosEndTimeHour - nowHours;
      var reMinutes = nextPosEndTimeMinutes - nowMinutes;
      var reSecond = 60 - nowSecond;
      //var day = 1 ;
      //var reHours = 24*day-nowHours-1;
      //var reMinutes = 60-nowMinutes-1;
      
      if(reHours< 10){//個位數+0
        document.getElementById("HH").innerHTML = "0" + reHours;
        document.getElementById("m_HH").innerHTML = "0" + reHours;
      }else{
        document.getElementById("HH").innerHTML = reHours;
        document.getElementById("m_HH").innerHTML = reHours;
      }
      
      if(reMinutes< 10){//個位數+0
        document.getElementById("MM").innerHTML = "0" + reMinutes;
        document.getElementById("m_MM").innerHTML = "0" + reMinutes;
      }else{
        document.getElementById("MM").innerHTML = reMinutes;
        document.getElementById("m_MM").innerHTML = reMinutes;
      }
      
      if(reSecond< 10){//個位數+0
        document.getElementById("SS").innerHTML = "0" + reSecond;
        document.getElementById("m_SS").innerHTML = "0" + reSecond;
      }else{
        document.getElementById("SS").innerHTML = reSecond;
        document.getElementById("m_SS").innerHTML = reSecond;
      }
      
      setTimeout("clock()",1000);
    }

    var saleStartTag = 0;
    function galist(){
      var result = '';
      
      var _data = {showType:1};
      momoj.ajax({
        url: '/ajax/promotionEvent_CustExclbuy.jsp',  //ETN
        async: false,
        cache: false,
        type: 'POST',
        dataType: 'text',
        contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=Big5',
        data: _data,
        timeout: 30000,
        success: function(rtnData){
          result = rtnData;
        },
        error : function(err, msg1, msg2){
          alert("ERROR\n很抱歉!伺服器暫時無法連線，請稍候再試");
        }
      });
      document.getElementById("CustExclbuy").innerHTML = result;
      return result;
    }
    
    function exclBuyGetToday(){
      var now=new Date();
      y=now.getFullYear();
      m=now.getMonth()+1;
      d=now.getDate();
      m=m<10?"0"+m:m;
      d=d<10?"0"+d:d;
      return y+"/"+m+"/"+d;
    }

    function exclBuyGetYear(){
      var now=new Date();
      y=now.getFullYear();
      return y;
    }

    function exclBuyGetMonth(){
      var now=new Date();
      var m=now.getMonth()+1;
      return m;
    }

    function exclBuyGetNowTime(){
        var now = new Date();
        return now.getHours()+":"+now.getMinutes()+":"+now.getSeconds();
    }
    
    function chkimg(){
      var _nowMonth = exclBuyGetMonth();
      var _now_date = exclBuyGetToday();
      var _now_time = _now_date + ' ' + exclBuyGetNowTime();
      var imgUrlDomain = getImgUrl();
      momoj('#CustExclbuy').find('.MENTAL').each(function(){
        var oThis = $(this);
        oThis.find('.time').html(oThis.find('.time').html()+' 開搶');
        
        var saleImg1 = oThis.find('img[name=saleImg1]');
        var saleImg2 = oThis.find('img[name=saleImg2]');
        saleImg1.attr('src' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_shop-on.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg1.attr('srcout' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_soldout2.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg1.attr('srcon' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_shop-on.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg1.attr('srcoff' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_soldout.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg2.attr('src' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_shop-off.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg2.attr('srcout' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_soldout2.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg2.attr('srcon' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_shop-off.png?t=1525401200978');
        saleImg2.attr('srcoff' ,imgUrlDomain + 'btn_soldout.png?t=1525401200978');

        var thisPeriodTime = oThis.find('.dateTime > .period > span').text();
        var splitPeriodTime = thisPeriodTime.split('~');
        var eventYear = exclBuyGetYear();
        if(_nowMonth == 12 && splitPeriodTime[0].split('/')[0] == '01'){
          eventYear = (eventYear - 0) + 1;//現在12月，顯示01月，加1年。
        }

        var _time = eventYear + '/' + splitPeriodTime[0] + ':00';
        var _end_time = eventYear + '/' + splitPeriodTime[1] + ':00';

        var dateNowTime = Date.parse(_now_time);
        var dateTime = Date.parse(_time);
        var dateEndTime = Date.parse(_end_time);

        var isShow = true;
        if(dateNowTime< dateTime){
          saleImg1.attr('src' ,saleImg1.attr('srcoff'));
          saleImg2.attr('src' ,saleImg2.attr('srcoff'));
        }else if(dateNowTime > dateEndTime){
          isShow = false;
          oThis.hide();
          saleImg1.attr('src' ,saleImg1.attr('srcout'));
          saleImg2.attr('src' ,saleImg2.attr('srcout'));
          oThis.find('#gdsStock_1').text('0');
        }else{
          saleStartTag++;
          oThis.attr('id','posTag' + saleStartTag);
        }
        
        if(isShow){
          var menu_txt; //20200810-Autumn
          if(_time.startsWith(_now_date)){//當天不顯示日期，只有時間。
            menu_txt = oThis.find('.time span').text();
          }else{
            menu_txt = splitPeriodTime[0];
          }
          var menu_li = '<li class="Nav-slide"><a href="javascript:void(0);" >' + menu_txt + '<i></i></a></li>';
          $('.fix_box_wrp').append(menu_li);//20200810-Autumn+ PC
          $('.Nav-wrapper').append(menu_li);//20200810-Autumn+ MB
        }

        //個別庫存對應顯示邏輯
        var olistLi = oThis.find('ul[class="product_Area"] > li');
        $.each(olistLi,function(index,element){
          var oLi = $(element);
          var stock = oLi.find('#gdsStock_1');
          var nowImg = oLi.find('#nowPImg_1');

          if(parseInt(stock.text())<= 0){
            var img1 = oLi.find('#saleImg1');
            var img2 = oLi.find('#saleImg2');

            img1.attr('src' ,img1.attr('srcout'));
            img2.attr('src' ,img2.attr('srcout'));
            nowImg.parent().addClass('imgout');
          }
        });

        if ( $(window).width() > 767 ) {
          momoj(this).find('.goShop').attr('class' , 'topnavArea');
        } else {
          momoj(this).find('.topnavArea').attr('class' , 'goShop');
        }
      });
        
      //20200302網址控制錨點
      var domainQur = window.location.search.substring(1); // domainQur = npn=1vEK1psAv1Uo&n=1&code=3
      if(domainQur !== ''){
       params = JSON.parse('{"'+ decodeURI(domainQur).replace(/"/g, '\\"').replace(/=/g, '":"').replace(/&/g, '","') +'"}');// {npn: 1vEK1psAv1Uo , n : 1, code : 3}
        //指定錨點 &tag=.Area_coupon_03 或 &tag=[id]Area_coupon_03   
        var npn = params.npn;
        //if( npn !== "1vEIzgmFCIpl"){
          params.tag = '[id]posTag1'
        //}
        var tag = params.tag;
        if(tag !== undefined) {
          tag = tag.replace('[id]','#');
          $(window).on('load',function(){
            if($(tag).offset()){ $('html,body').animate({scrollTop: $(tag).offset().top-50},300) };
          })
        }
      };
      
      $('#CustExclbuy .bottom_divArea > div').text('優惠商品數量有限，售完為止。本廣告活動頁商品規格、顏色、價位、贈品，momo購物網有權進行更改，以實際販售內容為主。');
    }
    function getImgUrl(){
      var edmImgUrl = '';
      momoj('img').each(function(){
        var thisImgSrc = momoj(this).attr('src');
        if(thisImgSrc.indexOf('/ecm/img/online/10/007/')>0){
          edmImgUrl = thisImgSrc;
          return false;
        }
      });
      if(edmImgUrl.indexOf('/images/')>0){
        edmImgUrl = edmImgUrl.substring(0,edmImgUrl.indexOf('/images/')+8);
      }
      return edmImgUrl;
    }
    momoj(document).ready(function(){
      galist();
      chkimg();
      clock();
    });

    $(function(){
      //copy時間標題
      $('#CustExclbuy').find('.MENTAL').each(function(){
        var oThis = $(this);
        oThis.find('.dateTime').after('<div class="dateTime_copy"></div>');
        oThis.find('.dateTime_copy').html($(this).find('.dateTime').html());
      });
    });

  <script>
   function waitingForBI() {
  var isBI = momoj().cookie('isBI');
  if(isBI != '1'){
    setTimeout(function(){
      waitingForBI();
    },500);
  } else {
    //有bid之後處理osm
    var osm = getUrlParameter('osm');
    var gid = getUrlParameter('gid_ic');
    var oid = getUrlParameter('oid');
    var i_code = getUrlParameter('i_code');
    var memid = getUrlParameter('memid');

    var data = {data:{URL:"/ajax/ajaxTool.jsp?rn=" + Math.random(), 
      flag:3099,
      "osm":osm,
      "gid_ic":gid,
      "oid":oid,
      "i_code":i_code,
      "memid":memid
      }}
    momoj.ajaxTool(data);
  }
}

var url = location.href;
if(url.indexOf('osm')>-1||url.indexOf('gid_ic')>-1||url.indexOf('oid')>-1||url.indexOf('memid')>-1){
  waitingForBI();//有bid之後處理osm
}

function getUrlParameter(name) {
    name = name.replace(/[\[]/, '\\[').replace(/[\]]/, '\\]');
    var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&]' + name + '=([^&#]*)');
    var results = regex.exec(location.search);
    return results === null ? '' : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
}
  </script>

    };
  }
